pack v

英音 pæk 美音 pæk

词频 4 | 口语 2 | 书面 1 | 阅读 0

英文释义

  1. 高义频： (把…) 打包；(把…) 装进 (箱子等) ：

Don’t forget to pack your toothbrush!
别忘了把牙刷放到箱子里去!

I haven’t packed yet.
我还没收拾行李呢。

packed their things / belongings
They hurriedly packed their things / belongings into the suitcase.
他们匆忙地把东西装进了行李箱。

  1. 高义频： 塞满；挤满：

More than two thousand students packed the hall.
两千多名学生把礼堂挤得满满的。

packed with
The bus was packed with people.
公共汽车上挤满了人。

packed into
We all packed into one car.
我们都挤进了一辆车里。

固定搭配

  • pack up

  1. 把…打包；收拾 (行李)：

Once a friend and I packed up some peanut butter and sandwiches for an outing.
有一次，我和一个朋友包好一些花生酱和三明治去郊游。

派生词汇

[null]

真题解析

题目

We were first greeted with the barking by a pack ____ dogs, seven to be exact.

答案 of
题目

The workers ____ (把…打包) the glasses and marked on each box “This Side Up”.

答案 packed

pain n

英音 peɪn 美音 peɪn

词频 4 | 口语 2 | 书面 2 | 阅读 0

用法点拨 [C] & [U]

英文释义

  1. 高义频： (肉体上的) 痛；疼痛：

have a pain in my stomach / stomach pains
I have a pain in my stomach / stomach pains.
我胃痛。

have pain all over
全身疼痛

  1. 高义频： (精神上的) 痛苦；苦恼：

cause (sb) pain
cause (sb) pain
使某人痛苦

The parents are still in great pain over the death of their child.
那对父母仍处于孩子离世带来的痛苦之中。

No pain, no gain.
不劳无获。

固定搭配

  • take pains to do sth

  1. 努力 / 下苦功做某事：

We should take pains to improve ourselves through learning and get prepared for the future.
我们应该通过学习努力改善自己，并为将来作好准备。

派生词汇

Learning English as a second language can be a painful experience.
把英语作为第二语言来学习时一段痛苦的经历。

My legs become painful.
我的腿开始疼了。

pair n

英音 peə(r) 美音 per

词频 4 | 口语 2 | 书面 2 | 阅读 0

用法点拨 [C]

英文释义

  1. 高义频： 一双 / 对；一把 / 副：

The shoes are too small for me. Show me another pair.
这鞋我穿着太小，再给我拿一双看看。

a pair of earrings / glasses / trousers / chopsticks
一对耳环/一副眼镜/一条裤子/一双筷子

一般可在pair前加定语。

a new pair of shoes
一双新鞋

a sharp pair of eyes
一双敏锐的眼睛

“a pair of +复数名词”作主语时，谓语动 词通常用单数形式。

A pair of gloves is a welcome present.
手套是一件受欢迎的礼物。

固定搭配

  • in pairs

  1. 成对地；两人一组地：

I want you to do this task in pairs.
我希望你们两人一组完成这项任务。

pardon n

英音 'pɑːdn 美音 'pɑːrdn

词频 2 | 口语 0 | 书面 0 | 阅读 0

用法点拨 [U]

英文释义

  1. 高义频： 原谅；宽恕：

begged her pardon for
He begged her pardon for arriving too late.
他来得太迟，请求她原谅。

固定搭配

  • I beg your pardon

  1. 高义频： [未听清对方的话，请求重复；常简化为 “beg pardon” 或 “pardon”] 什么；请再说一遍：

— You’re very quiet today.
你今天话很少啊。

— Pardon?
什么？

— I said you’re very quiet today.
我说你今天话很少。

  1. 低义频： [表示道歉] 对不起；请原谅：

I beg your pardon. I didn’t know this was your seat.
对不起，我不知道这座位是你的。

[null]

part n

英音 pɑːt 美音 pɑːrt

词频 5 | 口语 3 | 书面 3 | 阅读 0

用法点拨 [C]

英文释义

  1. 高义频： 部分；一部分：

divide the cheese into three equal parts
将奶酪分成三等份

a,part of
Music has become (a) part of my life.
音乐已经成为了我生活中的一部分。

an important part of
Vocabulary is an important part of language, just like bricks in a building.
词汇是语言的重要组成部分，正如盖楼的砖一样。

part前有形容词修饰时使用不定冠词，没有形容词修饰时通常不用冠词。

  1. 高义频： (机器的) 零件；(人、动植物的) 器官；部位：

spare parts
spare parts
备用零件

the parts of the body
身体各部位

  1. 高义频： [常用复数] 地区：

They try their best to find Olympic stamps issued by various parts of the world.
他们尽全力搜集世界各地发行的奥运邮票。

  1. 高义频： 角色：

play the part of
In the play, Adam will play the part of the leading role.
在剧中，亚当将扮演主角。

固定搭配

  • for the most part

  1. 通常；多数情况下：

For the most part, students work to earn money for their own use.
大多数情况下，学生打工赚钱是为了自己用。

  • in part

  1. 部分地；在某种程度上：

Some people said his success was due in part to luck.
有人说他成功的部分原因是运气好。

  • play / act a(n) (...) part (in)

  1. (在…中) 扮演角色 / 起作用：

Nowadays, the Internet plays an important part in our lives.
如今，互联网在我们的生活中起着重要作用。

  • take part (in)

  1. 参加；参与：

If Jim took part in the Talent Show, he’d win it for sure.
如果吉姆参加才艺大赛，他肯定会赢。

Eleven million students in Jiangsu took an active part in this program.
1100万江苏学生积极参与了这个项目。

take part in是固定搭配，part前一般不用冠词，但part前有形容词修饰时，要用不定冠词。

辨析 join, join in, take part in, attend

四者都常译为“参加”。

派生词汇

[null]

真题解析

[null]

part v

英音 pɑːt 美音 pɑːrt

词频 5 | 口语 0 | 书面 0 | 阅读 0

英文释义

  1. 低义频： (使) 分开；(使) 分离：

The long wall parts the city into two areas.
长长的城墙将城市一分为二。

The wind parted the smoke just enough for him to catch sight of Sibson.
风吹散了浓烟，刚好让他看见了希伯森。

  1. 低义频： 分手；告别：

We parted at the airport.
我们在机场告别。

固定搭配

  • part with

  1. (不情愿地) 放弃：

The novel is so attractive that I can’t stand parting with it.
这部小说引人入胜，我简直爱不释手。

particular adj

英音 pə'tɪkjələ(r) 美音 pər'tɪkjələr

词频 4 | 口语 3 | 书面 3 | 阅读 0

英文释义

  1. 高义频： [只用于名词前] 特定的
    used to emphasize that you are talking about one person, thing, time, etc. and not about others (specific)：

He did not show up on that particular day.
他并没有在那一天露面。

The giant panda eats only one particular type of bamboo.
大熊猫只吃某一种竹子。

  1. 高义频： 特别的；格外的：

nothing particular
I have nothing particular to do this evening.
今晚我没有什么特别的事要做。

We must pay particular attention to this point.
我们必须要特别注意这一点。

  1. 低义频： 讲究的；挑剔的：

a particular customer
挑剔的顾客

particular about / over
She is very particular about / over her appearance.
她很在意自己的外表。

固定搭配

  • in particular

  1. 尤其；特别：

Parents and coaches in particular should act as better examples for children.
父母和教练尤其要给孩子们树立更好的榜样。

Are you doing anything in particular this weekend?
这个周末你有什么特别的安排吗？

真题解析

[null]

pass v

英音 pɑːs 美音 pæs

词频 5 | 口语 3 | 书面 3 | 阅读 0

英文释义

  1. 高义频： 经过：

Please let me pass.
请让我过去。

She passes my house on her way to school.
她上学时路过我家。

  1. 高义频： 超过：

China passed the US to become the largest mobile phone market in the world.
中国超过了美国成为世界上最大的手机市场。

  1. 高义频： 通过 (考试、议案等)：

pass a law
pass a law
通过一项法律

To reach the goal, I must first try my best to pass the College Entrance Examination and enter a good university.
为实现这一目标，我必须先尽全力通过高考，考入一所好大学。

  1. 高义频： 度过 (时间)；(时间) 流逝：

pass the time
We sang songs to pass the time.
我们借唱歌来消磨时间。

Many years have passed, but I still remember it as if it were yesterday.
许多年过去了，但记忆中的一切仿佛就在昨天。

  1. 高义频： 递；传递：

  • pass sb sth / pass sth to sb:

Please pass me the book. / Please pass the book to me.
请把书递给我。

固定搭配

  • pass around / round

  1. 分发；传阅：

Pass the cookies around / round, would you?
请把小甜饼分发给大家，好吗？

  • pass away

  1. [委婉语] 去世；逝世：

He unfortunately passed away last year due to his cancer.
他去年因癌症不幸去世。

  • pass by

  1. 经过；(时间) 过去：

Did you see a man in black pass by just now?
你刚才有没有看见一位身穿黑色衣服的男子经过？

Three hours passing by, I became more and more impatient.
3小时过去了，我越来越不耐烦。

  • pass down

  1. 把…传下去 (hand down)：

She wants to be a gymnastics coach to pass down what she’s learned to other kids when she grows up.
她长大后想成为一名体操教练，把她所学的传授给其他孩子。

  • pass off as

  1. 把…冒充成：

He escaped by passing himself off as a guard.
他冒充警卫逃走了。

  • pass on

  1. 传递：

Please pass on the message to as many people as possible.
请将这个消息传达给尽可能多的人。

  • pass out

  1. 分发；分配；昏倒：

In the home for sick people, I helped wash clothes and sheets, and pass out lunch.
在患者之家，我帮忙洗衣服和床单，分发午餐。

I nearly passed out when I saw all the blood.
看到那么多血，我差点晕了过去。

  • pass through

  1. 穿过；通过

  • pass up

  1. 放弃；错过 (机会等)：

You shouldn’t pass up the opportunity to go to university.
你不该放弃上大学的机会。

派生词汇

passing interest
a passing interest / thought
一时的兴趣/想法

    反义词 impatient

was,patient with
She was usually patient with her students and never made them disappointed.
她对学生通常很有耐心，从来不让他们失望。

She has got used to the new patterns of family life.

a dress pattern

a pattern of dots

  1. 高义频： 模范；榜样：

pay n 重难点词汇

英音 peɪ 美音 peɪ

词频 5 | 口语 3 | 书面 3 | 阅读 0

用法点拨 [U]

英文释义

  1. 高义频： 工资；薪水：

low / high pay
low / high pay
低/高薪

辨析 pay, salary, wage

三者都可用作名词，含“报酬”之意，都常译为“工资”。

[null]

派生词汇

[null]

pay v 重难点词汇

英音 peɪ 美音 peɪ

词频 5 | 口语 3 | 书面 3 | 阅读 0

用法点拨 (paid, paid)

英文释义

  1. 高义频： 付 (钱)；支付：

  • pay sb sth:

I paid him 20 dollars to repair my bike.
我付给他20美元修自行车。

  • pay for sth:

I have to pay for the book lost.
我不得不为丢失的书支付赔偿金。

  • pay sth for sth:

He paid $2,000 for his new computer.
他买新电脑花了2000美金。

  • pay sb for sth:

Did Linda pay you for looking after her baby?
琳达付给你看孩子的钱了吗？

pay a bill
pay a bill
支付账单

a low-paid / well-paid job
低/高薪工作

paying in cash
— Are you paying in cash or by credit card?
你付现金还是刷信用卡?

pay cash
— I’ll pay cash.
我付现金。

辨析 cost, spend, pay, take

这四个词都经常译为“花费”，但用法各不相同。

  1. 高义频： 给予 (注意)；进行 (访问)：

pay attention to
pay attention to
注意

pay a visit to
pay a visit to sb / pay sb a visit
拜访某人

固定搭配

  • pay back

  1. 高义频： 偿还；报答：

Will you lend me $10? I’ll pay (it) back next month.
你借给我10美元好吗？我下个月还你。

That I can pay back the help people give me makes me happy.
能够回报人们给我的帮助让我感到很开心。

  1. 高义频： 报复：

Pay somebody back in his own coin.
以其人之道还治其人之身。

  • pay down

  1. 先支付 (部分货款) 作为定金

  • pay off

  1. 低义频： 还清 (欠债等)：

Once we’ve paid off the debts, we’ll owe money to no one.
一旦还清了债务，我们就不欠任何人的钱了。

  1. 高义频： 取得成功；得到好结果：

He studied hard before the examination, and it paid off. He made an A.
他在考试前努力学习，功夫没有白费，他得了个A。

  1. 低义频： 付清工资后解雇；遣散：

Over 1,000 workers will be paid off if this factory closes.
如果这家工厂关闭，会有超过1000名工人被解雇。

  • pay up

  1. (尤指不情愿或延迟) 付清欠款；偿还欠款

派生词汇

[null]

真题解析

题目

— Dad, I don’t think Oliver the right sort of person for the job.

— I see. I’ll go right away and pay him ____.

答案 off
题目

The watch was very good, and he paid 20 percent down ____ it.

答案 for
题目

The athlete’s years of hard training paid ____ when she finally won the Olympic gold medal.

答案 off

peace n

英音 piːs 美音 piːs

词频 4 | 口语 2 | 书面 2 | 阅读 0

用法点拨 [U]

英文释义

  1. 高义频： [可用单数] 和平：

peace talks
peace talks
和平会谈

The people of the world love peace.
世界人民热爱和平。

  1. 高义频： 平静；安宁
    the state of being calm：

peace of mind
Keeping on doing good deeds brings us peace of mind.
坚持做好事会给我们带来内心的平静。

  1. 高义频： 安静；清静
    the state of being quiet：

peace and quiet
The father wanted to be left alone to enjoy some peace and quiet.
那位父亲想一个人享受一下清静。

固定搭配

  • at peace

  1. 处于和平 / 平静状态：

The countries have been at peace for more than a century.
这些国家和平共处已有一个多世纪了。

Her mind is at peace.
她心境平和。

  • in peace

  1. 和平地；安宁地：

The two communities live together in peace.
这两个社区相安无事。

  • make (one’s) peace with

  1. 同…言归于好：

They finally made peace with each other after two weeks of arguing.
争吵了两周后，他们终于和好了。

Don’t promise anything unless you are one / a hundred percent (= completely) sure.
除非你有百分之百的把握，否则不要答应任何事。

“percent of + 名词 / 代词”作主语，名词 / 代词为复数时，谓语动词用复数；名词为不可数名词或代词为单数时，谓语动词用单数。

Ten percent of the students are absent today.
今天有10%的学生缺席。

About 30 percent of the land is covered in forest.
这片陆地约30%覆盖着森林。

permit v 重难点词汇

英音 pə'mɪt 美音 pər'mɪt

词频 4 | 口语 0 | 书面 1 | 阅读 0

用法点拨 [正式用语]

英文释义

  1. 高义频： 许可；准许
    to allow sth to happen or sb to do sth 反义词 forbid：

  • permit sb sth:

Please permit me a few words.
请允许我说几句。

  • permit sb to do sth:

He permitted me to retake the test, and I pulled my grade to an A.
他允许我重新参加考试，我的成绩因此提高到了A。

permitted,in
Mobile phone conversations are not permitted anywhere in the library.
图书馆内任何地方都禁止使用手机打电话。

  1. 高义频： (使) 成为可能：

if time permits
I’ll pick you up at the airport if time permits.
如果时间允许的话，我会去机场接你。

weather permitting
We’ll start tomorrow, weather permitting (= if the weather is good enough).
天气允许的话，我们明天出发。

permit you to
Cash machines permit you to withdraw money at any time.
取款机可以让你随时取款。

permit和allow的用法相似，permit是正式用语；指天气、时间等客观因素允许时，只能用permit。

persuade vt 重难点词汇

英音 pə'sweɪd 美音 pər'sweɪd

词频 4 | 口语 1 | 书面 2 | 阅读 0

英文释义

  1. 高义频： 说服；劝服 (talk into)：

  • persuade sb to do sth:

She persuaded me to go to a dental school.
她说服了我去牙科学校学习。

  • persuade sb into (doing) sth:

I managed to persuade my classmates into accepting my idea.
我设法说服了我的同学接受我的想法。

  • persuade sb out of (doing) sth:

We persuaded him out of his foolish plan.
我们说服了他放弃那项愚蠢的计划。

She is always easily persuaded.
她总是很容易被说服。

在表示“劝说”，但不一定“劝服”时，用try to persuade。

She would try to persuade local business leaders to contribute money to the cause.
她会劝说当地的商界领导人为该事业捐款。

  1. 高义频： 使相信；使信服 (convince)：

  • persuade sb of sth:

I’m persuaded of his honesty.
我相信他是诚实的。

  • persuade sb + that 从句:

I persuaded him that I was telling the truth.
我使他相信我讲的是实情。

固定搭配

[null]

pick vt 重难点词汇

英音 pɪk 美音 pɪk

词频 5 | 口语 3 | 书面 3 | 阅读 0

英文释义

  1. 高义频： 摘；采：

pick grapes / flowers
采摘葡萄/采花

  1. 高义频： 摘掉；剔除：

pick one’s teeth
剔牙

He picked the nuts off the top of the cake.
他把蛋糕上面的果仁拿掉。

  1. 高义频： 挑选；选择：

  • pick sb to do sth:

When I was in the third grade, I was picked to be the princess in the school play.
在三年级时，我被选为校园剧中的公主。

  • pick sb / sth for sth:

Ben was picked for the soccer team.
本被选进了足球队。

picked,words
He picked his words carefully.
他用词细心谨慎。

辨析 select, choose, pick

三者都有“选择”之意。

固定搭配

  • pick sb’s pocket

  1. 扒窃；掏包

  • pick on

  1. 挑选；故意挑剔：

Why do you pick on me to do the unpleasant jobs?
你为什么找我做这些令人不愉快的工作?

Why pick on my family?
为什么拿我的家庭说事？

  • pick out

  1. 高义频： 选出；拣出：

Perhaps you can help me pick out a pair of jeans, since you are an expert.
因为你是个行家，也许你能帮我挑选一条牛仔裤。

His story was picked out as the best by the judges.
他的小说被评委们评为最佳作品。

  1. 低义频： 区别出；辨别出：

See if you can pick me out in this photo.
看你能不能从这张照片上认出我来。

There have been experiments where people could pick out a particular smell.
有实验证明，人们可以辨认出某种特定的气味。

  • pick up

  1. 高义频： 提起；拿起：

  • 拿起；拾起：

The phone rang and I picked it up.
电话响了，我接了起来。

I picked up the rubbish and threw it into the trash can.
我把垃圾拾起来，扔进垃圾桶。

She went over to the crying child and picked her up.
她走到啼哭的孩子身边，把她抱了起来。

  • (车辆等) 中途搭 (人) (collect)；中途带 (货)：

I’ve got to pick up my daughter from school at four o’clock.
我四点钟得去学校接女儿。

Buses pick up and drop off people at different places on the route.
公交车在其线路上不同的地方让人们上下车。

  • 营救；救起：

Twenty men fell into the water and were picked up by other boats.
二十人落水后，被其他船只救起。

  1. 高义频： 得到：

  • (偶然地、无意地) 得到 / 买到；学会 (语言)：

pick up bad habits
染上了坏习惯

He picked up a few dollars by doing part-time jobs.
他靠兼职挣了几个钱。

She picked up Japanese when she was in Japan. Now she can speak it freely.
她在日本的时候学会了日语，现在她日语讲得很流利。

We managed to pick up a few bargains in the market.
我们从市场上买到了几件便宜货。

  • 接收到：

We were able to pick up the BBC World Service.
我们能收听到英国广播公司的国际广播节目。

  1. 高义频： 取回；收集：

I’ll pick up the tickets at lunchtime tomorrow.
我明天午饭时间去取票。

pick up the heat
收集热量

  1. 低义频： 重提 (话题)；恢复 (状态等)：

He picks up this theme again in later chapters of the book.
在该书的后几章，他又重回到这个主题上。

things are picking up
We’ve been through a hard time, but things are picking up again now.
我们经历了一段困难的日子，不过现在情况又好转了。

  1. 低义频： 提高；(风) 变大：

picked up speed
The train picked up speed.
火车提速了。

The wind had picked up, and dark clouds rolled across the sky.
风愈刮愈大，天空中乌云密布。

派生词汇

[null]

真题解析

题目

It’s surprising that your brother picked ____ Russian so quickly — he hasn’t lived there very long.

答案 up
题目

Sam picked ____ some knowledge of the computer just by watching others working on it.

答案 up
题目

It was so dark in the cinema that I could hardly pick ____ my friend.

答案 out

你不能来真是遗憾。

[null]

place n

英音 pleɪs 美音 pleɪs

词频 5 | 口语 3 | 书面 3 | 阅读 0

用法点拨 [C]

英文释义

  1. 高义频： 地方；地点；部位：

Birds seek safe places before a storm.
鸟儿会在暴风雨来临前寻找安全的地方。

a sore place on the leg
腿上的疼痛处

  1. 高义频： 住所；场所：

my place
Some of my friends are coming for dinner at my place.
有几个朋友要来我家吃饭。

  1. 低义频： 位置；地位；身份：

Working has a very important place in all our lives.
工作在我们生活中占据着重要位置。

  1. 低义频： 资格；名额；机会：

get a place in a law firm
在律师事务所工作

They might just have a place left on the writing course.
写作课或许正好还有一个剩余名额。

  1. 高义频： 名次：

Luck was smiling on me that day as I won first place in the competition.
那天幸运女神向我微笑，我获得了比赛第一名。

固定搭配

  • in place

  1. 在适当的位置；适当的；准备妥当：

The ropes hold you in place so that you don’t fall.
绳子会把你固定在适当的位置，这样你就不会掉下去。

After the dinner, an expression of thanks to the host would be in place.
饭后向主人道声谢是比较合适的。

The service could be in place by the end of the year.
这项服务将于年底准备就绪。

  • in place of

  1. 代替；取代 (in sb’s / sth’s place)：

You can use yoghurt in place of cream to make this salad.
你可以用酸奶替代奶油来做这道沙拉。

If I refused to go, they would send someone else in my place.
如果我不去，他们会派其他人代替我的。

  • out of place

  1. 不在合适的位置上；不合适的；不相称的：

Some of these files seem to be out of place.
有些文件似乎没放对地方。

I felt completely out of place among all these successful people.
夹在这些成功人士中间，我觉得自己格格不入。

  • take place

  1. 发生；举行：

Great changes have taken place in the way people communicate in recent years.
近年来，人们交流的方式发生了巨大的变化。

辨析 happen, take place

二者都可指“发生”。

  • take the place of

  1. 代替 (take sb’s / sth’s place):

Computers have taken the place of typewriters in offices.
在办公室里，电脑已取代了打字机。

She couldn’t attend the meeting so her assistant took her place.
她不能出席会议，所以她的助手代替了她。

派生词汇

[null]

真题解析

[null]

place vt

英音 pleɪs 美音 pleɪs

词频 5 | 口语 3 | 书面 3 | 阅读 0

英文释义

  1. 高义频： 放置；安置：

He placed his fingers on the piano keys.
他把手指放在钢琴键上。

  1. 高义频： 发出 (订单)；登 (广告)：

place,order,advertisement
place an order / advertisement
下订单/登广告

  1. 低义频： 定名次：

He was placed third in last Saturday’s race.
在上周六的比赛中，他名列第三。

固定搭配

[null]

派生词汇

[null]

真题解析

题目

The furniture, with its modern style and bright colors, suits modern houses and their gardens, but looks ____ (不相称的) in the garden of a traditional home.

答案 out of place

plain adj

英文释义

  1. 高义频： 清楚的；明白的；易懂的 (clear / obvious)：

The story is written in plain English.
故事用简单易懂的英语写成。

  1. 高义频： 简朴的；简单的；单色的
    without anything added or without decoration：

a plain but elegant dress
朴素淡雅的连衣裙

plain yoghurt
原味酸奶

The bike is in plain black and easy to ride.
这辆自行车是纯黑色的，非常好骑。

  1. 低义频： 平常的；相貌平平的：

a policeman in plain clothes
便衣警察

Her face is plain, but she has a nice smile!
她长相普通，但笑容很甜美！

  1. 高义频： 坦白的；直率的：

Let us be plain with you.
我们坦白对你说吧。

play v

英音 pleɪ 美音 pleɪ

词频 5 | 口语 3 | 书面 3 | 阅读 0

用法点拨 vt & vi

英文释义

  1. 高义频： 做 (游戏)；玩耍；娱乐：

Show us how to play the game, will you?
你能教我们怎么玩这个游戏吗？

The streets I used to play in are jammed with cars now.
我过去经常玩耍的街道如今堵满了汽车。

playing with
Kathy picked up a lot of Spanish by playing with the native boys and girls.

This scene doesn’t play so well.
这一场演得并不好。

  1. 高义频： 播放 (唱片、磁带等)：

Play their new CD for me, please.
请把他们的新唱片放给我听一下吧。

  • play with

  1. 玩弄：

pleasure n

英音 'pleʒə(r) 美音 'pleʒər

英文释义

  1. 高义频： [U] 快乐 (enjoyment)；娱乐：

took pleasure in
From her teenage years, she took pleasure in writing short stories.
从十几岁起，她就喜欢写些小故事。

  1. 高义频： [C] 乐事；乐趣：

Giving is always a pleasure.
给予永远都是件乐事。

a,pleasure to
It is a great pleasure to meet you students from England.
非常高兴认识你们这些从英国来的学生。

他享受生活中所有的乐趣。

固定搭配

  • for pleasure

  1. 作为消遣：

We read mainly for information, not for pleasure.
我们读书主要是为了获取信息，并非为了消遣。

  • it’s a pleasure / (it’s) my pleasure

  1. [用于对别人感谢的回答] 别客气；没什么：

— Thank you for coming to help us.
谢谢你来帮助我们。

— It’s a pleasure. / My pleasure.
别客气。

  • with pleasure

  1. 高兴地；[用于应答] 非常乐意：

Invited into a friend’s home, you should accept with pleasure.
如果被邀请去朋友家做客，你应该高兴地接受。

— Would you like to come and have lunch on Sunday?
你愿意周日来吃午餐吗？

— With pleasure. I’d love to come.
当然了，我很乐意来。

point v 重难点词汇

英音 pɔɪnt 美音 pɔɪnt

词频 5 | 口语 2 | 书面 2 | 阅读 0

英文释义

  1. 高义频： [不用于被动语态] 用 (手指等) 指；指向：

  • point at / to / towards sb / sth:

It is rude to point your finger at others.
用手指指他人是不礼貌的。

  1. 高义频： 对准：

pointed at
A hundred cameras were being pointed at her.
上百个相机对准了她。

  1. 高义频： 面向；朝向：

points in a,direction
The sign post points in a wrong direction.
路标指向错误的方向。

points to / towards
The needle of a compass always points to / towards the north.
罗盘的指针总指向北。

  1. 低义频： (意思上) 指向；暗示；表明：

pointed to / towards
All the evidence pointed to / towards Tony as the thief.
所有证据都表明托尼是小偷。

固定搭配

  • point out

  1. 把…指出来 (给看)；指出；指明：

pointed out to
I pointed out to him where I used to live.
我把我过去住的地方指给他看。

pointed out that
He pointed out that the road was not safe in winter.
他指出这条路冬天不安全。

派生词汇

[null]

真题解析

[null]

point n 重难点词汇

英音 pɔɪnt 美音 pɔɪnt

词频 5 | 口语 3 | 书面 3 | 阅读 0

英文释义

  1. 高义频： [C] 尖端；点；小数点：

the point of a pencil / knife
铅笔尖/刀尖

The two lines cross at point C.
这两条线在C点相交。

two point six
二点六(2.6)

  1. 高义频： [C] 时间点；地点：

a turning / starting point
a turning / starting point
转折点/起点

a low / high point
a low / high point
低谷/巅峰

at some point
You’ll regret at some point in the future if you don’t study hard today.
如果你现在不好好学习，将来某个时候你就会后悔。

reached a point
I have reached a point in my life when / where I am supposed to make decisions of my own.
我到了人生中应该自己拿主意的时候。

  1. 高义频： [C] 观点；要点；特点：

from,point of view
Whenever you buy a present, you should think about it from the receiver’s point of view.
每当你买礼物时，都应当从接受者的角度来考虑。

main points
Read the passage and get the main points of it.
阅读这篇文章并理解其要点。

that’s not the point
You didn’t intend to be late. But that’s not the point (= not the important thing).
你不想迟到，但那不是重点。

make,point
He told a story, within which he tried to make his point.
故事中他提出了自己的观点。

strong / weak points
strong / weak points
强项/不足处

  1. 高义频： [C] (比赛或运动中的)分 (数)：

win a match by ten points to three
以10比3赢得比赛

  1. 高义频： [U] 意图；目的；理由
    the purpose or aim of sth：

What’s the point
What’s the point of forcing him to do what he is unwilling to?
强迫他做不愿意做的事情有什么意义呢?

There’s no point in
There’s no point in getting angry.
生气是没有用的。

固定搭配

  • make a point of doing sth

  1. (即使费力也) 特意做某事：

He made a point of spending Saturdays with his children.
星期六他必定要和孩子们在一起。

  • on the point of

  1. 正要…的时候：

She was on the point of going out when the telephone rang.
她正要出去，电话铃响了。

  • to the point

  1. 中肯的；切题的：

Your advice is very much to the point.
你的建议很中肯。

get to the point
I wish you’d get to the point (= talk about the most important thing).
我希望你能切入正题。

[null]

一个人的食物对于另一个人来说可能是毒药。/ 萝卜白菜，各有所爱。

poor adj

英音 pɔː(r); pʊə 美音 pɔːr

词频 5 | 口语 3 | 书面 3 | 阅读 0

英文释义

  1. 高义频： 贫穷的；贫困的；贫乏的
    反义词 rich

as poor as a church mouse
一贫如洗

the poor
穷人

poor in
That country is poor in natural resources.
那个国家自然资源匮乏。

  1. 高义频： 不善于的；差的；体弱的：

in poor health
He was in poor health.
他身体不好。

poor at
I am poor at sports.
我不擅长运动。

  1. 高义频： 可怜的；不幸的：

The poor man lost both his legs in the accident.
这个不幸的人在事故中失去了双腿。

固定搭配

[null]

派生词汇

真题解析

It is difficult to figure out a global population of polar bears as much of the range has been ____ (poor) studied.

popular adj 重难点词汇

英音 'pɒpjələ(r) 美音 'pɑːpjələr

词频 5 | 口语 2 | 书面 3 | 阅读 0

英文释义

  1. 高义频： 流行的；受欢迎的
    反义词 unpopular：

increasingly popular
Online voting becomes increasingly popular, and many competitions get people involved in it.
在线投票越来越盛行，很多比赛都让人们参与进来投票。

  • be popular with / among

  1. 为…喜欢；受…欢迎：

The mobile phone is fashionable and convenient to carry, so it is very popular with youngsters.
这款手机样式新颖、携带方便，深受年轻人的欢迎。

Smart and pretty, Kate is very popular among her friends.
凯特既聪明又漂亮，深受朋友们的喜爱。

  1. 高义频： 公众的；大众化的；通俗的：

a popular belief / opinion
a popular belief / opinion
普遍的观念/民意

What we need most are popular science books.
我们最需要的是科普类图书。

in popular language
用通俗的语言

固定搭配

[null]

派生词汇

[null]

真题解析

题目

This magazine is very popular ____ young people, who like its content and style.

答案 with / among

population n 重难点词汇

英音 ˌpɒpju'leɪʃn 美音 ˌpɑːpju'leɪʃn

词频 4 | 口语 2 | 书面 3 | 阅读 0

用法点拨 [C]

英文释义

  1. 高义频： 人口；人口数量：

a country with the ageing population
人口老龄化的国家

The Bai ethnic group has a population of around two million, 90% of whom live in Yunnan.
白族人口大约有200万，其中的90%居住在云南。

  1. 高义频： (某事物的) 总数；(人的) 全体：

the dolphin population
海豚总数

The whole population of the town came out to welcome him.
整个镇上的居民都出来欢迎他。

问“…有多少人口？”时，要使用what，不能用how many或how much；修饰人口多少的形容词不用many或few，而用large或small。

What is the population of Zhejiang Province?
浙江省有多少人口？

China has the largest population in the world.
世界上中国人口最多。

固定搭配

[null]

派生词汇

[null]

真题解析

题目

The population of Jiangsu ____ to more than twice what it was in 1949. The figure is now approaching 74 million.

A.has grown
B.have grown
C.grew
D.are growing

答案 A

position n 重难点词汇

英音 pə'zɪʃn 美音 pə'zɪʃn

词频 4 | 口语 3 | 书面 3 | 阅读 0

英文释义

  1. 高义频： 位置；方位；(恰当或正确的) 位置：

Can you show me the position of the city on the map?
你能在地图上给我指出那个城市的位置吗？

in position
The orchestra were all in position, waiting for the conductor.
管弦乐队队员都已各就各位，等待着指挥。

  1. 高义频： 姿势；(物体所指的) 方向：

comfortable position
Lie in a comfortable position.
以一种舒适的姿势躺下。

They had to stand for hours without changing position.
他们得一动不动地站几个小时。

Keep the box in an upright position.
把盒子竖着放。

  1. 高义频： 地位；身份：

The,position of
The social position of each character influences the way they behave to each other.
每个人的社会地位影响他们对待彼此的方式。

a man of position
有身份的人

  1. 高义频： [正式用语] 职位；职务 a job (post)：

applying for,position
He is thinking of applying for the position of Chief Editor.
他正在考虑申请主编的职位。

takes / holds,position
Bruce takes / holds the position of sales manager in a large company.
布鲁斯在一家大公司担任销售经理的职务。

  1. 低义频： (比赛中的) 名次：

finished,in third position
She finished the race in third position.
她在比赛中得了第三名。

  1. 高义频： 处境；状况
    the state or situation that sb / sth is in：

in,position
What would you do if in my position?
如果处于我这种状况你会怎么办？

not in a position
I’m afraid I am not in a position to help you.
我恐怕帮不了你。

  1. 高义频： 立场；观点；态度
    an opinion on or an attitude towards a particular subject (attitude)：

take,position on
When the time comes to make a decision and take a position on an issue, allow for the contributions of each member of the group.
就某个问题作出决定和发表意见的时候，要允许组内每个成员提出自己的想法。

reconsider,position
I hope you’ll reconsider your position.
我希望你能重新考虑你的立场。

派生词汇

真题解析

题目

There is no possibility ____ Bob can win the first prize in the match.

答案 that

 

possible adj

英音 'pɒsəbl 美音 'pɑːsəbl

词频 5 | 口语 3 | 书面 3 | 阅读 0

英文释义

  1. 高义频： 可能的
    反义词 impossible:

  • it is possible (for sb) to do sth:

It is possible for him to accomplish the task.
他有可能完成这项任务。

  • it is possible + (that) 从句：

It is possible that we have met before.
我们可能以前见过。

Anything is possible.
一切皆有可能。

  1. 高义频： 合理的；可接受的
    reasonable or acceptable in a particular situation：

There are several possible explanations.
有几种合理的解释。

  1. 低义频： [用于形容词后表示强调] 最...的：

best possible
It was the best possible surprise anyone could have given me.
那是我曾感受过的最大的惊喜。

last possible
Don’t leave your packing until the last possible moment.
别把打点行李拖到最后一刻。

固定搭配

  • as ... as possible

  1. 尽可能...地：

Try to make your poster as attractive as possible.
使你的海报尽可能地吸引人。

We must take action as quickly as possible now.
我们现在必须尽快采取行动。

You have to search for as many opportunities as possible to practice listening.
你要寻找尽可能多的机会练习听力。

  • if possible

  1. 如果可能的话：

I want to avoid the rush hour traffic if possible.
如有可能，我想避开交通高峰期。

  • whenever / wherever possible

  1. 只要有可能；一有机会：

Use public transport whenever possible (= when you can).
只要有可能，就用公共交通工具。

power n 重难点词汇

英音 'paʊə(r) 美音 'paʊər

词频 5 | 口语 3 | 书面 3 | 阅读 0

英文释义

  1. 高义频： 能力；[可用复数] (生理) 机能：

do everything in my power
I will do everything in my power to help you.
我会尽全力帮助你。

power of speech
After the accident she lost the power of speech.
那次事故后，她失去了说话能力。

The drug may affect your powers of concentration.
这种药可能会影响你的注意力。

  1. 高义频： 力量；威力：

Every storm is an example of the power of nature.
每场暴风雨都是大自然威力的例证。

辨析 force, energy, strength, power

四者都有“力”、“力量”之意，但具体意思不同。

  1. 高义频： 控制力；影响力：

power over
Once you are confident about your power over bad situations, problems are just stepping stones to success.
一旦你对自己掌控恶劣局势的能力感到自信，难题就是你迈向成功的垫脚石。

He made the mistake of underestimating the power of the press.
他犯的错误是低估了新闻界的影响力。

  1. 高义频： 统治；政权：

in power
a political party in power
执政党

came to power
The party came to power at the last election.
这个政党是在上次大选中上台执政的。

  1. 高义频： 权力；职权：

More than fame or fortune, she wanted power.
她对权力的渴望甚于名声和财富。

  1. 高义频： 大国；强国：

an industrial power
工业大国

world powers
world powers
世界强国

  1. 高义频： 动力；电力；功率：

wind / nuclear / solar power
wind / nuclear / solar power
风/核/太阳能

power station
a power station
发电站

power failure / cut
a power failure / cut
停电

engine power
engine power
发动机功率

practice n 重难点词汇

英音 'præktɪs 美音 'præktɪs

词频 5 | 口语 2 | 书面 3 | 阅读 0

英文释义

  1. 高义频： (反复) 训练；练习：

Practice makes perfect
Practice makes perfect.
熟能生巧。

John is at baseball practice.
约翰正在进行棒球训练。

To learn English well requires a lot of practice.
学好英语需要大量的练习。

  1. 高义频： 实践；实际行动：

We must combine theory with practice.
我们必须把理论与实践相结合。

  1. 高义频： 惯例；习惯做法；习俗
    the usual or expected way of doing sth; a habit or custom：

according to the international practice
按照国际惯例

The practice of students endlessly copying letters and sentences from a blackboard is a thing of the past.
学生们没完没了地从黑板上抄写单词和句子的做法是过去的事了。

Customs are common social practices.
习俗指的是普遍的社会惯常做法。

固定搭配

  • in practice

  1. 实际上；事实上：

Your suggestion is very good in theory, but in practice it will not work.
理论上，你的建议很好，但实际上，是行不通的。

  • out of practice

  1. 生疏；疏于练习：

If you don’t play, you’ll get out of practice.
不练习就会生疏。

  • put ... into practice

  1. 将…付诸实践：

She’s been able to put a lot of what she’s learnt into practice in her home.
她在自己家里已经能实践很多自己学到的东西。

predict vt

英音 prɪ'dɪkt 美音 prɪ'dɪkt

词频 4 | 口语 0 | 书面 1 | 阅读 3

英文释义

  1. 高义频： 预言；预计 (forecast)：

  • predict + (that) / wh- 从句：

Population experts predict that most people will live in cities in the near future.
人口专家预言，在不久的将来大多数人都会住到城市里。

It’s hard to predict when driverless cars will be everywhere on our roads.
很难预料何时我们的公路上才会出现大量的无人驾驶汽车。

  • it is predicted + that 从句：

It was predicted that inflation would continue to fall.
据预测，通货膨胀率将继续下降。

predict tomorrow’s weather
预告明天的天气

[null]

prefer vt 重难点词汇

英音 prɪ'fɜː(r) 美音 prɪ'fɜːr

词频 5 | 口语 2 | 书面 2 | 阅读 0

用法点拨 (preferred, preferred)

英文释义

  1. 高义频： 更喜欢；更愿意：

  • prefer sb / sth to do sth:

I’d prefer you to start early.
我更希望你早点出发。

I prefer my English classes to be taught in English only.
我希望我的英语课是全英语授课。

  • prefer to do sth / doing sth:

Some people prefer to do almost everything over the Internet.
有些人喜欢在网上做几乎一切事情。

I prefer shutting myself in and listening to music all day on Sunday.
周日我喜欢一整天把自己关在屋里听音乐。

  • prefer (doing) sth to (doing) sth:

I prefer the red dress to the green one because it fits me better.
比起那条绿裙子，我更喜欢那条红色的，因为它更适合我。

I would prefer reading books to watching television.
比起看电视，我还是喜欢读书。

  • prefer + that 从句：

They preferred the money (should) be used for building schools and hospitals.
他们更愿意拿这笔钱来建学校和医院。

I would prefer that you didn’t mention my name.
我希望你不要提到我的名字。

— Tea or coffee?
喝茶还是咖啡？

— I’d prefer tea, thanks.
我更喜欢茶，谢谢。

She prefers her coffee black.
她更喜欢喝清咖啡。

prefer + that 从句结构中，从句中用虚拟语气。

固定搭配

[null]

派生词汇

按优先顺序

  1. 高义频： 偏爱的事物 / 人：

Wine or beer? Which is your preference?
葡萄酒还是啤酒？你更喜欢哪种？

他们正忙着筹备婚礼。

prepare v 重难点词汇

英文释义

  • prepare sth / sb for sb / sth:

正在为这位客人准备一间旅馆客房。

The lectures help students prepare for college mathematics.

    to give sth to sb, especially formally at a ceremony：

    to show or offer sth for other people to look at or consider：

principle n

英音 'prɪnsəpl 美音 'prɪnsəpl

词频 3 | 口语 2 | 书面 3 | 阅读 1

英文释义

  1. 高义频： 原理；原则
    the basic idea that a plan or system is based on：

basic principle
the basic principle
基本原理/基本原则

guiding principle
Excellent customer service should be our guiding principle.
优秀的客户服务应该成为我们的指导原则。

  1. 高义频： 道德准则；行为准则
    a moral rule or belief about what is right and wrong, that influences how you behave：

man of principle
a man of principle
有原则的人

it’s against my principles
I refuse to lie about it; it’s against my principles.
我绝不为此事撒谎，那有悖我的原则。

on principle
She’d never ask to borrow money, on principle.
原则上，她从不向别人借钱。

  1. 高义频： (机器等的) 工作原理；(自然界的) 定律；法则
    a general or scientific law that explains how sth works or why sth happens：

Archimedes’ principle
阿基米德定律

These machines both work on the same principle.
这两台机器的工作原理是相同的。

固定搭配

  • in principle

  1. 高义频： 理论上；原则上：

I agree with it in principle but I doubt if it will happen in practice.
理论上我同意，但是不知道实际上能否可行。

  1. 高义频： 大体上；基本上：

We agree with it in principle but we still need to discuss the details.
我们大体上同意，但是仍需讨论细节。

派生词汇

[null]

真题解析

题目

Anyway, I can’t cheat him — it’s against all my ____ (原则).

答案 principles

 

print v

英音 prɪnt 美音 prɪnt

词频 4 | 口语 2 | 书面 1 | 阅读 0

英文释义

  1. 高义频： 打印；印刷：

print the document
打印文件

Six thousand copies of the book are printed.
这本书印了6 000册。

  1. 高义频： 刊登 (publish)：

It is his wish that his stories would be printed in local newspapers.
他希望自己的故事会刊登在当地报纸上。

  1. 高义频： 印 (照片)：

It usually takes a couple of hours for the pictures to be developed and printed.
冲印照片通常需要几个小时。

固定搭配

  • print off / out

  1. 打印：

You may use an online printer to print out the data.
你可以使用网络打印机把数据打印出来。

problem n

英音 'prɒbləm 美音 'prɑːbləm

词频 5 | 口语 3 | 书面 3 | 阅读 0

用法点拨 [C]

英文释义

  1. 高义频： 问题；难题：

health / family problems
health / family problems
健康 / 家庭问题

cause / solve a problem
cause / solve a problem
引起 / 解决问题

I’ve been having problems with
I’ve been having problems with my computer system.
我的电脑系统一直有问题。

  1. 低义频： (考试、教科书中的) 问题：

She set her pupils many mathematical problems.
她给学生们布置了很多数学题。

固定搭配

  • no problem

  1. 高义频： [表示乐于相助或事情容易做]没问题：

— How about meeting at the nearby restaurant?
在附近的餐馆见面如何？

— No problem.
没问题。

  1. 高义频： 没关系；不客气：

— Thanks for the ride.
谢谢你载我一程。

— No problem.
不客气。

辨析 problem, question

二者都可译作“问题”。

用法点拨 [C]

英文释义

  1. 高义频： 过程；进程：

It's the process not the end product that matters.
重要的是过程，而不是最终结果。

a,slow process
Getting fit is a long slow process.
恢复健康是个漫长的过程。

in the process of
We’re still in the process of moving house.
我们还正在搬家呢。

  1. 高义频： 工序；步骤：

This was the first stage of the printing process.
这是印制过程的第一道工序。

固定搭配

  • in the process

  1. 同时：

I spilt the coffee, burning myself in the process.

produce vt

英音 prə'djuːs 美音 prə'duːs

词频 5 | 口语 3 | 书面 3 | 阅读 0

英文释义

  1. 高义频： 产生；引起
    to cause a particular result or effect (bring about)：

Giving sometimes produces nice results.
给予有时会产生好的结果。

Childhood experiences produce far-reaching effect on the health of grown-ups.
儿时的经历对成年后的健康会产生深远的影响。

  1. 高义频： 生产；创作
    to make, write etc. sth to be bought, used or enjoyed by people：

mass-produce
In 1914 Henry Ford began to mass-produce cars using assembly lines.
1914年亨利·福特开始使用流水线大量生产汽车。

produce,from
Each year, world-famous artists are invited to design and produce works of art from the ice.
每年，一些世界闻名的艺术家都被邀请来用冰块设计和创作艺术作品。

  1. 高义频： 出产；生育：

Australia has produced some famous painters and world-class writers.
澳大利亚出了一些著名画家和世界级的作家。

He had a cow which produced milk every day.
他有一头奶牛，每天都产奶。

  1. 低义频： 监制；制作 (电影、戏剧等)：

In the last few years thousands of films have been produced all over the world.
过去几年中，全世界制作了数千部电影。

[null]

promise v 重难点词汇

英音 'prɒmɪs 美音 'prɑːmɪs

词频 5 | 口语 2 | 书面 2 | 阅读 0

英文释义

  1. 高义频： 许诺；保证；答应：

  • promise to do sth:

The new monitor promised to do the best she could for us all.
新班长承诺会为我们大家竭尽全力。

  • promise (sb) + (that) 从句:

I promise that you will get all your money back.
我保证你会拿回你所有的钱。

  • promise sb sth / promise sth to sb:

She has been promised a new bike.
有人答应给她买辆新自行车。

I’ve promised the book to Susan.
我已经答应把这本书给苏珊了。

— She’s not coming tonight.
她今晚不来了。

— But she promised.
但她答应过的。

  1. 低义频： 有...的希望；有...的可能：

  • promise to be sth:

It promises to be a fine day.
天气有望好转。

Those clouds promise rain tomorrow.
那些云预示着明天有可能下雨。

propose v 重难点词汇

英音 prə'pəʊz 美音 prə'poʊz

词频 2 | 口语 2 | 书面 2 | 阅读 1

英文释义

  1. 高义频： [正式用语] 提出；提议；建议
    to formally suggest sth as a possible plan or action：

  • propose doing sth:

The report proposes extending motorways.
该报告建议拓宽机动车道。

  • propose + that … (should) do sth:

A professor at the Academy has proposed that a fund (should) be established to raise money.
学院的一位教授提议设立基金会来募集资金。

propose a better solution
提出更好的解决方案

  1. 高义频： [正式用语] 打算；计划
    to intend to do sth：

  • propose doing / to do sth:

He proposed buying / to buy a new car.
他打算买一辆新车。

  1. 高义频： 求婚：

proposed marriage
I’ve proposed marriage to her.
我已经向她求婚了。

protect v

英音 prə'tekt 美音 prə'tekt

词频 5 | 口语 2 | 书面 2 | 阅读 0

英文释义

  1. 高义频： vt & vi 保护；防护：

  • protect sb / sth from sth:

We put a sheet of plastic across the floor to protect us from the damp.
我们在地板上铺了一块塑料膜以防潮。

Something must be done to protect the environment from being polluted.
必须采取措施以保护环境免受污染。

  • protect (sb / sth) against sth:

Physical exercise can protect you against heart disease.
体育锻炼可以预防心脏病。

Waxing your car will help protect against rust.
给车打蜡可以防止生锈。

protect the earth
保护地球

辨析 defend, guard, protect

  1. 三者都含有“保护”之意。 固定搭配

他很爱护他的弟弟。

proud adj

英音 praʊd 美音 praʊd

词频 4 | 口语 2 | 书面 1 | 阅读 0

英文释义

  1. 高义频： 骄傲的；自豪的
    反义词 ashamed ：

  • (be) proud of sb / sth:

We are very proud of ourselves and believe we can do more for a better world.
我们非常自豪，并相信为了让世界更美好，我们可以做得更多。

  • (be) proud to do sth:

She is proud to have taken part in competitions and to have broken a record.
她对自己参加比赛并打破了纪录感到自豪。

  • (be) proud + that 从句：

She was proud that her daughter had so much talent.
女儿这么有天赋，她很自豪。

a proud look
得意的表情

  1. 高义频： [含贬义] 妄自尊大的；自负的：

She is too proud to see her own mistake.
她太自负了，看不到自己的错误。

固定搭配

[null]

prove v 重难点词汇

英音 pruːv 美音 pruːv

词频 5 | 口语 2 | 书面 3 | 阅读 0

用法点拨 (proved, proved / proven)

英文释义

  1. 高义频： 证明；证实：

  • prove sth to sb:

Just give me a chance and I’ll prove it to you.
给我一个机会，我会证明给你看。

表示向某人证明某事时应该用prove sth to sb，而不能用prove sb sth。

  • prove sb / sth (to be) + adj / n:

They put me in prison, but, in the end, I was proved innocent.
他们把我关进监狱，但我最终被证明是清白的。

He proved himself (to be) a better driver than the world champion.
他证明了自己的驾驶技术胜过世界冠军。

  • prove + that / wh-从句：

Sarah wants to prove that she has brains as well as beauty.
萨拉想证明她既有美貌，又有头脑。

The challenge proved how difficult it is to drive across a desert without guidance.
这个挑战证明在没有引导的情况下开车穿越沙漠是多么的困难。

  • it is proved that:

It has been proved that eating vegetables in childhood helps to protect you against serious illnesses in later life.
经证实，童年时吃蔬菜有助于日后不生大病。

  • prove oneself (to sb):

When I first started this job, I felt I had to prove myself.
我刚开始干这份工作的时候，觉得必须证明一下自己的实力。

prove his point
Riis believed that poverty caused crime, and he used photos to help him prove his point.
理斯认为贫穷导致犯罪，他还借助照片来证明自己的观点。

  1. 高义频： [用作系动词] 证明是；被发现是 (turn out)：

  • prove+adj/n:

The book has proved very successful.
事实证明了这本书非常成功。

  • prove to be sth

He proved to be an honest friend.
事实表明他是一个诚实的朋友。

固定搭配

[null]

派生词汇

[null]

真题解析

题目

To ____ (证明) his point, Professor Brown mentioned several other experiments which had similar results.

答案 prove

provide vt 重难点词汇

英音 prə'vaɪd 美音 prə'vaɪd

词频 5 | 口语 3 | 书面 3 | 阅读 0

英文释义

  1. 高义频： 提供；供应：

  • provide sth for sb:

Community schools provide good quality education for children.
社区学校为孩子们提供高质量的教育。

  • provide sb with sth:

The job will provide me with a good chance to show my talent.
这份工作将为我提供展示自己才华的好机会。

  • provide sth to sb:

This is a group that specializes in providing housing and services to needy people.
这是一个专门为有需求的人提供住房和服务的团队。

Working out in the morning provides additional benefits beyond being physically fit.
晨练不仅能保持身体健康，还能给我们带来其他的好处。

固定搭配

  • provide for

  1. 低义频： 抚养；供养：

She needs her new, busy work to provide for her family.
她的新工作很繁忙，但她需要它来养家糊口。

  1. 低义频： 为...作准备；防备：

We did not provide for such a great increase in prices.
我们没有为如此之大的价格涨幅作准备。

辨析 provide, offer, supply

三者都有“供给、提供”的意思，但用法不同。

派生词汇

provided /prə'vaɪdɪd/ conj

provided,that
I will play tennis provided (that) we’re finished by 5 pm.
要是我们5点结束，我就去打网球。

英文释义

  1. 高义频： [只用于名词前] 大众的；公众的：

a danger to public health

The media has a powerful influence on public opinion.

public transport / transportation

用法点拨 [与the连用]

英文释义

The news shocked the public, leading to great concern about students’ safety at school.
这则消息使公众感到震惊，同时引起人们对学生在校安全的极大关注。

the public作主语时，如表示整体，谓语动词用单数形式；如表示各个成员，谓语动词用复数形式。

  • in public

  1. 当众；公开地【反:in private】：

Don’t laugh or talk loudly in public. It’s bad manners.
不要在公共场合大声说笑，这样不礼貌。

pull v

英音 pʊl 美音 pʊl

词频 5 | 口语 3 | 书面 3 | 阅读 0

用法点拨 vt & vi

英文释义

  1. 高义频： 拉；拖：
    反义词 push

Pull,open
Pull the door open. Don’t push it.
把门拉开，不要推。

She pulled the chair towards her.
她把椅子拖到自己身边。

辨析 draw, drag, pull

三者均可表示“拉”。

  1. 高义频： 拔 (出)；抽 (出)：

She has to have two teeth pulled.
她必须拔掉两颗牙。

  1. 低义频： (使) (车、船等) 移动：

The bus pulled to a stop.
公共汽车停了下来。

  1. 低义频： 吸引：

The commercial pulled young people to the new product.
这则广告引起了年轻人对这款新产品的关注。

固定搭配

  • pull away

  1. 驶离；离开：

The traffic lights went green and I pulled away.
交通灯变绿，我开车离开。

  • pull down

  1. 把…往下拉；拆毁：

Pull down your hat so that nobody will recognize you.
把帽子拉低，这样就没人能认出你。

The old building has been pulled down for safety reasons.
考虑到安全因素，那座旧楼被拆毁了。

  • pull in / into

  1. (列车等) 进站；(汽车等) 靠边停下

  • pull off

  1. 把…驶离大路；成功完成

  • pull on

  1. 穿；戴 (袜子、手套等)：

Pull on gloves when you go out.
外出时戴上手套。

  • pull out

  1. 高义频： 拉出；拿出：

He pulled out a mobile phone and made a call.
他掏出手机打了个电话。

  1. 高义频： (列车等) 出站
  1. 高义频： (为超车而) 驶离车辆行列：

A car suddenly pulled out in front of me.
一辆汽车突然从侧面冲到我前面。

  1. 低义频： (使) 退出；(使) 撤离：

Most of the troops have been pulled out.
大部分军队已撤离。

  • pull over

  1. (使) 停靠在路边

  • pull through

  1. (使) 恢复健康；(使) 渡过难关：

The doctor said I was not going to pull through.
医生说我无法康复了。

  • pull together

  1. 组合；整顿；同心协力

  • pull up

  1. (使) (车等) 停下：

A car pulled up behind me.
一辆车停在我后面。

purpose n 重难点词汇

英音 'pɜːpəs 美音 'pɜːrpəs

词频 5 | 口语 2 | 书面 2 | 阅读 3

英文释义

  1. 高义频： 目标；目的
    the intention or aim of sth：

purpose of
What’s the purpose of your visit to London?
你去伦敦的目的是什么？

For the purpose of
For the purpose of helping protect Grand Canyon, please follow the guidelines below.
为了有助于保护大峡谷，请遵守如下准则。

Work gives you meaning and purpose and life is empty without it.
工作给了你意义和目标。没有工作的人生是空虚的。

  1. 高义频： 用途；作用
    the function of sth：

serve no purpose
Tears serve no purpose.
眼泪无济于事。

serve / answer the same purpose
I haven’t got a pen, but a pencil can serve / answer the same purpose.
我没带钢笔，不过用铅笔也一样。

  1. 高义频： 用意；需要
    what is needed in a particular situation：

for medical purposes
Using animals for medical purposes should be avoided.
应避免用动物做医学实验。

  1. 高义频： 意义：

sense of purpose
Volunteer work gives her life a sense of purpose.
志愿者工作让她的生活有了意义。

固定搭配

  • on purpose

  1. 故意地；有意地 (deliberately)
    反义词 by accident：

Cinderella left her shoe on the stairs on purpose.
灰姑娘故意把自己的鞋落在楼梯上。

派生词汇

purposeful /'pɜːpəsfl/ adj purposely /'pɜːpəsli/ adv

真题解析

push v

英音 pʊʃ 美音 pʊʃ

词频 4 | 口语 3 | 书面 3 | 阅读 0

英文释义

  1. 高义频： 推 (动) 【反:pull】；按下 (press)：

pushed,open
She pushed the door open and showed the doctor in.
她推开门把大夫领了进来。

pushed,back
She pushed her hair back from her forehead.
她把头发从前额往后拨。

push the button
按下按钮

  1. 高义频： 挤；推挤：

pushed through
We pushed through the crowd.
我们从人群中挤过。

pushed their way into
They pushed their way into the train looking for seats.
他们挤上火车寻找座位。

  1. 高义频： 劝说；鼓励：

  • push sb into (doing) sth:

My teacher pushed me into entering the competition.
我的老师鼓励我参加比赛。

  1. 低义频： 逼迫；催促：

push,to the extreme limit
Athletes push themselves to the extreme limit of their body to complete the over 42 kilometers race.
要完成超过42公里的赛程，运动员需要把自己的体能发挥到极限。

Set your alarm clock an hour early and push yourself to work out!
把你的闹钟调前一小时，强迫自己去锻炼。

固定搭配

  • push aside

  1. 推开；排挤；设法忘掉：

Just when she was about to speak, a student rushed in and pushed her aside!
正当她要讲话时，一个学生冲了进来将她推到一边。

She pushed aside her anger, forcing herself to focus on her work.
她抛开愤怒，强迫自己专心工作。

  • push on

  1. 继续前进；继续 (做某事)：

Let’s push on; it’s nearly nightfall.
咱们继续走吧，天快黑了。

  • push over

  1. 推倒；(风) 刮倒：

The big tree was pushed over by the wind.
这棵大树被风刮倒了。

派生词汇

[null]

Encourage your children to try new things, but try not to ____ (逼迫) them too hard.

Give,a push

真题解析

[null]

put vt

英音 pʊt 美音 pʊt

词频 5 | 口语 3 | 书面 3 | 阅读 0

用法点拨 (put, put)

英文释义

  1. 高义频： 放 (置) (place)；安装；把...送往：

Put a little more sugar in this coffee, will you?
请再往这杯咖啡里加点糖，好吗？

I had to put a new lock on the door.
我只好给门安装了新锁。

In 1969 the Americans put a man on the moon.
1969年美国人把人类送上了月球。

  1. 高义频： 写上；标上；注上：

put in
I couldn’t read what she had put in the diary.
我看不懂她日记里写了什么。

  1. 高义频： 说；表达：

put it another way
He was too trusting — or, to put it another way, he had no head for business.
他太轻信人了，换句话说，他没有商业头脑。

Put simply
Put simply, we accept their offer or go bankrupt.
简言之，我们要么接受他们的条件，要么破产。

As,put it
As news report put it, when women joined the organization it took on a new look.
正如报道所言，女性加入那个组织后，其面貌焕然一新。

  1. 低义频： 提出：

put a question
提出一个问题

  1. 高义频： 使处于 (某种状态)：

Put yourself in my position
Put yourself in my position. What would you have done?
站在我的立场，你会怎么办？

All of these pressures put teens in a terrible situation.
所有这些压力把青少年置于一个艰难的处境。

  1. 低义频： 认为；把…视为：

put,among
I put Hemingway among my favourite authors.
我将海明威视为我最喜爱的作家之一。

put,before
I put my family before my job.
我把家庭看得比工作重要。

put sb / sth first
put sb / sth first
把某人 / 某事物放在首位

固定搭配

  • put aside

  1. 低义频： 把...放在一边；把...撇开不理：

She put the newspaper aside and stood up.
她把报纸放到一边站了起来。

You must put aside your pride and apologize to him.
你必须放下自尊向他道歉。

  1. 低义频： 储存钱备用：

They put some money aside every month for their retirement.
他们每月都存些钱供退休后用。

  • put away

  1. 高义频： 把...收起；放好：

Kids — will you put away your toys now?
孩子们，现在把玩具收起来好吗？

  1. 低义频： 储存...备用：

We’re putting some money away for expenses.
我们省下一笔钱来应付开销。

  1. 低义频： 抛弃；放弃 (想法等)：

Put your worries away and enjoy life.
别再担心了，好好享受人生吧！

  • put back

  1. 高义频： 把...放回原处；使...恢复原状：

Please put back the books and magazines when you’ve finished with them.
阅读完书和杂志后请放回原处。

  1. 高义频： 推迟； 延迟 (postpone)：

Because of the bad weather, the voyage was put back twelve hours.
由于天气恶劣，起航推迟了12个小时。

  • put down

  1. 高义频： 放下：

Once I started reading the mystery novel, I just couldn’t put it down.
一旦我开始读那本疑案小说，就再也放不下了。

put the bag down
把包放下

  1. 低义频： 写下；记下 (write down)：

Please put down your name and address here.
请把您的姓名和地址写在这儿。

  1. 低义频： 付 (订金)；批评

  • put forward

  1. 把…提前；提出 ; 推荐 :

We have put forward the wedding by two weeks.
我们把婚礼提前了两周。

Who put forward a theory about black holes?
谁提出了黑洞理论？

  • put in

  1. 低义频： 插入 (意见、话语等)；投入 (时间、金钱等)：

Holly is always putting in her unwanted opinions.
霍莉总是插嘴，发表些没用的见解。

If you’re not willing to put in the time and work, don’t expect to receive any rewards.
如果你不愿投入时间和付出劳动，不要指望得到任何回报。

  1. 低义频： 把...添进 (信函、故事等)：

If you’re writing to your mother, don’t forget to put in something about her coming to stay.
你要是正给你母亲写信,可别忘了加上几句请她来住上几天。

  1. 高义频： 安装；配备；种植：

The school has put in many new computers for the students’ use.
学校配备了许多新电脑供学生使用。

She has put in 15 tomato plants, and five rows of a variety of vegetables.
她种了15株西红柿和5垅各色蔬菜。

  • put into

  1. 把…投入；(使) 进入… (状态)；把…翻译成：

Nothing is difficult in the world if you put your heart into it.
世上无难事，只怕有心人。

put into effect
These suggestions were adopted and put into effect.
这些建议被采纳，并付诸实施。

Put this sentence into English.
把这个句子译成英语。

  • put off

  1. 高义频： 延期；推迟 (delay / postpone)：

She called this afternoon to put off the meeting to next week.
她下午打电话说把会议推迟到下周。

  1. 高义频： 使反感；使不信任：

She is very clever but her manner does tend to put people off.
她很聪明，但态度令人反感。

  1. 高义频： 打扰；使分心：

Don’t put me off when I’m trying to concentrate.
在我想要集中精力的时候别打扰我。

  1. 高义频： 使对...失去兴趣：

Don’t let your failures put you off trying harder.
别因为失败你就不再进一步努力了。

  • put on

  1. 高义频： 穿上；戴上【反:take off】；抹：

Remember to put on more clothes to keep warm.
记得多穿点衣服保暖。

Protect your skin — put on sunscreen right as you head outside.
保护好你的皮肤，外出时要搽上防晒霜。

辨析 wear, put on, dress

三者均可作“穿”解，但意义、用法不同。

  1. 高义频： 使运转；播放：

I put on the car flashlights and drove on at a really low speed.
我打开车灯，以很慢的速度向前行驶。

I didn’t see him but I heard him put on his favourite CD.
我没看见他，但听到他播放他最喜欢的CD了。

  1. 高义频： 增加 (gain)：

put on,weight
He’s put on a lot of weight.
他的体重增加了很多。

  1. 低义频： 上演 (戏剧等)：

We once put on a performance of Hamlet.
我们曾表演过《哈姆雷特》。

  1. 低义频： 征收 (税金等)；施加 (压力)；将...归咎：

put a tax on
征税

They put pressure on her to resign.
他们向她施加压力，让她自动请辞。

He put the blame for his failure on me.
他把自己的失败归咎于我。

  • put out

  1. 高义频： 把...拿出去：

put the rubbish / garbage out
清理垃圾

  1. 高义频： 把...准备好：

The girls helped her to put out the cups and plates.
姑娘们帮她把茶杯和盘子摆好。

  1. 高义频： 熄灭；扑灭：

The firemen came and put out the fire.
消防员来把火扑灭了。

  1. 低义频： 伸出 (手、脚等)：

The doctor asked me to put out my tongue.
医生叫我伸出舌头。

  1. 低义频： 出版；公布；广播：

They put out a half-hour programme on Chinese kongfu.
他们播出了一档半小时的关于中国功夫的节目。

I put out a request for volunteers for my kids' club.
我为孩子们所在的俱乐部发布了志愿者需求公告。

辨析 go out, put out

二者都和“熄灭”有关。

  • put through

  1. 低义频： 使经受 (困难或令人不悦的事情)：

I told myself I would not put my mom through that pain again.
我告诉自己不能再让妈妈经受那样的痛苦了。

  1. 低义频： 安排某人上学；供某人上学：

She worked as a waitress to put herself through college.
她当服务员挣钱来供自己上大学。

  1. 高义频： 为...接通电话；接通 (电话)：

Could you put me through to the manager, please?
请帮我接通经理的电话，好吗？

  • put together

  1. 组装；组建；拼凑出：

It took us all morning to put the proposal together.
我们花了一上午的时间整理出这份建议。

  • put up

  1. 高义频： 举起；抬起；提高：

Put up your hands if you have any questions.
如果有问题请举手。

They have put up the rent by $200 a month.
他们把每月的租金提高了200美元。

We put up an umbrella to keep the water off when it rains.
下雨时我们撑开雨伞来遮挡雨水。

  1. 高义频： 公布；张贴 (布告、相片等) (display)：

Posters were put up around our school, calling upon us to join in the actions for a greener earth.
校园中到处张贴着海报，号召我们加入到让地球更环保的行动中去。

  1. 高义频： 建造 (房屋等)；搭建：

They’ve put up a lot of high-rise buildings recently.
最近他们盖起了很多高楼大厦。

  1. 高义频： 留宿；住宿：

I was hoping Kenny could put me up for a few days.
我希望肯尼能让我留宿几天。

  • put up with

  1. 忍受；容忍 (tolerate)：

I can’t put up with their smoking any longer.
我再也无法忍受他们抽烟了。

I can put up with many things, but not with people who steal.
我能容忍很多事情，但绝不容忍小偷小摸的人。

真题解析

题目

At the last moment, Tom decided to put ____ a new character to make the story seem more likely.

答案 in
题目

Mary is really good at taking notes in class. She can put _____ almost every word her teacher says.

答案 down
题目

The exam results will be put _____ on Friday afternoon.

答案 up
题目

I can put up ____ the house being untidy, but I hate it if it’s not clean.

答案 with
题目

He decided that he would drive all the way home instead of ____ at a hotel for the night.
A.putting down
B.putting off
C.putting on
D.putting up

答案 D
题目

My mother opened the drawer to put _____ the knives and spoons.

答案 away
题目

Just as Professor Scotti often ____ it, success is ninety-nine percent mental attitude.
A.gets
B.makes
C.puts
D.means

答案 C
题目

Don’t be so discouraged. If you put ____ such feelings, you will do better next time.

答案 away

 

puzzle n

英音 'pʌzl 美音 'pʌzl

词频 4 | 口语 0 | 书面 0 | 阅读 0

英文释义

  1. 高义频： 难题；谜；拼图游戏：

Why Mona Lisa is smiling is still a puzzle.
蒙娜丽莎为什么微笑仍然是个谜。

puzzle vt

It puzzles scientists how these creatures can survive in such severe conditions.
这些生物是如何在这样艰难的条件下存活的，这使科学家很疑惑。
